href=\"/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/ctr_anim_latest.gif\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/ctr_anim_latest.gif\" alt=\"Control\" data-animated-image=\"\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e (territorial control)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/map_anim_latest.gif\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/map_anim_latest.gif\" alt=\"All events\" data-animated-image=\"\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e (events)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eVIINA/ВІЙНА/ВОЙНА/WAR 2.0 is a near-real time multi-source event data system for the 2022 Russian Invasion of Ukraine. These data are based on news reports from Ukrainian and Russian media, which were geocoded and classified into standard conflict event categories through machine learning. In addition to raw events, VIINA also includes data on territorial control, at the level of individual populated places.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThese data are GIS-ready, with temporal precision down to the minute. Each observation is accompanied by full source information, text and URLs.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eVIINA is updated daily, and is freely available for use by students, journalists, policymakers, and everyday researchers under an \u003ca href=\"#open-data-commons-open-database-license\"\u003eOpen Database License (ODbL)\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe most recent versions these data are available as a comma-delimited-text (csv) files within the following compressed ZIP archives:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca locations)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/control_latest_2023.zip\"\u003eData/control_latest_2023.zip\u003c/a\u003e | Territorial | De-duplicated event reports and labels for 2025 (\"one-per-day\" filter)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote that each event data release includes both raw event reports (\u003ccode\u003eevent_info\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003eevent_labels\u003c/code\u003e) and a simplified, de-duplicated data file (\u003ccode\u003eevent_1pd\u003c/code\u003e). The latter uses a \"one-per-day\" filter to remove potential duplicate event reports, by treating multiple event reports of the same type (i.e. same combination of actor and tactic labels) in the same populated place on the same day as a single unique event.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003ePrevious data versions are available by request (email me).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAlso included are tessellated geometries of Ukrainian populated places, which were used to create some of the maps on this site. These can be matched to the territorial control data by the variable \u003ccode\u003egeonameid\u003c/code\u003e (\u003ccode\u003econtrol*\u003c/code\u003e datasets) or \u003ccode\u003ekod\u003c/code\u003e (\u003ccode\u003ekontrol*\u003c/code\u003e datasets):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/gn_UA_tess.geojson\"\u003eData/gn_UA_tess.geojson\u003c/a\u003e  (N = 33,141 populated places)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/katotth_UA_tess.geojson\"\u003eData/katotth_UA_tess.geojson\u003c/a\u003e  (N = 29,724 populated places)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eFor additional information on VIINA (1.0) and illustrative analyses, see:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eZhukov, Yuri (2023). \"Near-Real Time Analysis of War and Economic Activity during Russia’s Invasion of Ukraine.\" \u003cem\u003eJournal of Comparative Economics\u003c/em\u003e 51 (4): 1232-1243 (\u003ca href=\"https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jce.2023.06.003\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003edoi.org/10.1016/j.jce.2023.06.003\u003c/a\u003e). dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#territorial-control\"\u003eTerritorial control data and sources\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#event-data-sources\"\u003eEvent data sources\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"#geocoding\"\u003eEvent data href=\"#codebook\"\u003eEvent data variable names\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eTerritorial Control Data\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-territorial-control-data\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Territorial Control Data\" href=\"#territorial-control-data\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/map_ctr_latest.png\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\"/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/map_ctr_latest.png\" alt=\"Current status\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eVIINA data on territorial control are based on four sources:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eVIINA event reports on territorial control\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePolygon map layers from DeepStateMap (Ukraine)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePolygon map layers from Institute for the Study of War (U.S.)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eCrowdsourced control maps from Wikipedia\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eIn cases where these data sources disagree, a \"majority vote\" rule is used to determine whether a populated place is under the control of Ukrainian forces, Russian forces, or is being actively contested between the two. If these \"votes\" are evenly split, ties are broken in favor of DeepStateMap.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote that Institute for the Study of War (ISW) territorial control data are updated less frequently than the other three sources.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eTerritorial control data are available for two sets of geographic units.\nThe first (\u003ccode\u003econtrol\u003c/code\u003e) includes full set of Ukrainian populated places in the \u003ca href=\"https://www.geonames.org/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eGeoNames gazetteer\u003c/a\u003e (N = 33,141), with feature_code's beginning in PPL*.\nThe second (\u003ccode\u003ekontrol\u003c/code\u003e) uses Ukraine's national register of administrative divisions, \u003ca href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Codifier_of_administrative-territorial_units_and_territories_of_territorial_communities\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eKATOTTH\u003c/a\u003e (N = 29,724), which can be more easily merged with official government statistics.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEach territorial control dataset includes the following fields:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003egeonameid\u003c/code\u003e (in \u003ccode\u003econtrol*\u003c/code\u003e datasets only): Numeric ID of populated place (can be linked to geometries in \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/gn_UA_tess.geojson\"\u003egn_UA_tess.geojson\u003c/a\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ekod\u003c/code\u003e (in \u003ccode\u003ekontrol*\u003c/code\u003e datasets only): KATOTTH code of populated place (can be linked to geometries in \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/katotth_UA_tess.geojson\"\u003ekatotth_UA_tess.geojson\u003c/a\u003e)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003edate\u003c/code\u003e: Date of map update (YYYYMMDD)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003estatus_wiki\u003c/code\u003e: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from Wikipedia crowdsourced maps\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003estatus_boost\u003c/code\u003e: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from Wikipedia \"boosted\" by VIINA event reports\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003estatus_dsm\u003c/code\u003e: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from DeepStateMap\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003estatus_isw\u003c/code\u003e: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from Institute for the Study of War\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003estatus\u003c/code\u003e: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), \"majority vote\" of wiki, boost and dsm\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003evcontrol_version\u003c/code\u003e: Date and time of VIINA territorial control data release\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eNote that the structure of these data have recently changed. Starting October 13, 2024, the data files are split by calendar year. Each yearly file follows the same \"long\" panel data format (rows are daily observations for each populated place, columns are control status from different sources).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv portal\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://zona.media/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eМедиазона\u003c/a\u003e (\"mz\"): Russian news portal\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca Газета\u003c/a\u003e (\"ng\"): Russian newspaper\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.ntv.ru/novosti/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eНТВ\u003c/a\u003e (\"ntv\"): Russian television news\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.pravda.com.ua/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eУкраїнська правда\u003c/a\u003e (\"pravdaua\"): Ukrainian newspaper\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://ria.ru/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eРИА Новости\u003c/a\u003e (\"ria\"): Russian news wire service\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.unian.info/\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eУНІАН\u003c/a\u003e (\"unian\"): Ukrainian news wire service\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThis set of sources may expand/change as the war unfolds -- due to interruptions to journalistic activity from military operations, cyber attacks, and state censorship, as well as the availability of new data from other information providers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eUsing an automated web scraping routine (which runs every 6 hours), VIINA extracts the text of news reports published by each source and their associated metadata (publication time and date, web urls). Using natural language processing, the system extracts and geocodes location names mentioned in each news item. A neural network model then classifies each event report into several pre-defined categories.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eGeocoding\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-geocoding\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Geocoding\" href=\"#geocoding\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eEvents were geo-located by place names mentioned in the text of each news report, using APIs from Yandex and OpenStreetMaps. All unique geocoded locations were manually inspected for false positive and false negative matches.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eGeocoding precision ranges from street-level (\u003ccode\u003eGEO_PRECISION=\"STREET\"\u003c/code\u003e) to province-level (\u003ccode\u003eGEO_PRECISION=\"ADM1\"\u003c/code\u003e).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBelow is a map of \u003cstrong\u003eall\u003c/strong\u003e geocoded event reports since the start of Russia's military operations on February 24, 2022. Underneath the map is a timeline, showing the number of event reports published per day, across all data sources.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener potential duplicates (\u003ccode\u003eevent_1pd_latest.csv\u003c/code\u003e):\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" about military operations, with one-a-day filter\" style=\"max-width: 100%;\"\u003e\u003c/a\u003e (reports about military operations, one-per-day filter)\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eEvent classification\u003c/h2\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-event-classification\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Event classification\" href=\"#event-classification\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe data currently include the following event categories:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_mil\u003c/code\u003e: Event is about war/military operations\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_loc\u003c/code\u003e: Event report includes reference to specific location\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_san\u003c/code\u003e: Event report mentions economic sanctions imposed on Russia\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea_rus\u003c/code\u003e: Event involves Russian or Russian-aligned armed forces\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea_ukr\u003c/code\u003e: Event involves Ukrainian or Ukrainian-aligned armed forces\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea_rus_init\u003c/code\u003e: Event initiated by Russian or Russian-aligned armed forces\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea_ukr_init\u003c/code\u003e: Event initiated by Ukrainian or Ukrainian-aligned armed forces\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea_civ\u003c/code\u003e: Event initiated by civilians\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003ea_other\u003c/code\u003e: Event initiated by a third party (e.g. U.S., EU, Red Cross)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_aad\u003c/code\u003e: Anti-air defense, Buk, shoulder-fired missiles (Igla, Strela, Stinger)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_airstrike\u003c/code\u003e: Air strike, strategic bombing, helicopter strike\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_uav\u003c/code\u003e: Unmanned or remotely-piloted aerial vehicle\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_airalert\u003c/code\u003e: Air raid siren/alert\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_armor\u003c/code\u003e: Tank battle or assault\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_arrest\u003c/code\u003e: Arrest by security services or detention of prisoners of war\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_artillery\u003c/code\u003e: Shelling by field artillery, howitzer, mortar, or rockets like Grad/BM-21, Uragan/BM-27, other Multiple Launch Rocket System (MRLS)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_control\u003c/code\u003e: Establishment/claim of territorial control over population center\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_firefight\u003c/code\u003e: Any exchange of gunfire with handguns, semi-automatic rifles, automatic rifles, machine guns, rocket-propelled grenades (RPGs)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_ied\u003c/code\u003e: Improvised explosive device, roadside bomb, landmine, car bomb, explosion\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_raid\u003c/code\u003e: Assault/attack by paratroopers or special forces, usually followed by a retreat\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_occupy\u003c/code\u003e: Occupation of territory or building\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_property\u003c/code\u003e: Destruction of property or infrastructure\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_cyber\u003c/code\u003e: Cyber operations, including DDOS attacks, website defacement\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_hospital\u003c/code\u003e: Attacks on hospitals and humanitarian convoys\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_milcas\u003c/code\u003e: Event report mentions military casualties\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003et_civcas\u003c/code\u003e: Event report mentions civilian casualties\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eVIINA 2.0 uses a BERT-based transformer model (\u003ca href=\"https://doi.org/10.48550/arXiv.1810.04805\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eDevlin, et al., 2018\u003c/a\u003e) to classify news headlines into the above event categories. Transformers, first developed by Google in 2017, are a class of neural networks that can provide significant performance and efficiency gains over previous generations of recurrent neural networks (RNNs) and convolutional neural networks (CNNs) by using attention, which tracks relationships between elements of the data and enabling significant parallelization. One high-performing and widely-utilized transformer model is Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers (BERT), developed by Google in 2018. This model uses only transformer encoder layers, whereas other models make use of both encoders and decoders, or only decoders.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWe employ an iteration of the BERT-base model, pre-trained using 12 transformer layers, 110 million parameters, and 3.3 billion words. Specifically, we use \u003ca href=\"https://huggingface.co/KoichiYasuoka/bert-base-slavic-cyrillic-upos\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eKoichiYasouka's bert-base-slavic-cyrillic-upos model\u003c/a\u003e, an iteration of the \u003ca href=\"https://huggingface.co/ai-forever/ruBert-base\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eruBERT\u003c/a\u003e-base model trained on Belarusian, Bulgarian, Russian, Serbian, and Ukrainian texts for part-of-speech tasks. We fine-tune this model for classification using a labeled random subset of the Ukrainian and Russian news headlines scraped for VIINA and use the resulting fully-trained model to categorize all VIINA headlines.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe previous version of VIINA (1.0) used an RNN model with long short-term memory (LSTM) (\u003ca href=\"https://doi.org/10.1162/neco.1997.9.8.1735\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eHochreiter and Schmidhuber, 1997\u003c/a\u003e). LSTMs are well-suited for learning problems related to sequential data, such as sequences of words of differential length, where the vocabulary is potentially large, and where the long-term context and dependencies between inputs are potentially informative for classification (i.e. where word order and context matters, and the bag-of-words assumption is problematic).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBelow is a comparison of out-of-sample classification accuracy statistics --- areas under the Receiver-Operator Characteristic (AUC ROC) curves --- for the BERT (\u003ccode\u003eroc_bert\u003c/code\u003e) and LSTM (\u003ccode\u003eroc_lstm\u003c/code\u003e) models. These statistics can be interpreted as the probability that the model assigns a higher predicted probability to a randomly chosen event (e.g. \u003ccode\u003et_mil=1\u003c/code\u003e) than to a randomly chosen non-event (e.g. \u003ccode\u003et_mil=0\u003c/code\u003e). An AUC of 1 indicates perfect out-of-sample accuracy. An AUC of 0.50 indicates that a model performs no better than random classification. AUCs can be particularly useful in evaluating predictive performance for categories with high class imbalance (i.e. rare events, with a lot of 0's and very few 1's).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs the table suggests, BERT universally dominates LSTM on this metric:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"left\"\u003evariable\u003c/th\u003e\n\u003cth align=\"right\"\u003e0.9991970\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"right\"\u003e0.5052192\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"left\"\u003et_retreat\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"right\"\u003e1\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"right\"\u003e0.9918534\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"right\"\u003e0.4949084\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"left\"\u003et_airalert\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"right\"\u003e5\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"right\"\u003e0.8078029\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003ctd align=\"right\"\u003e0.7219713\u003c/td\u003e\n\u003c/tr\u003e\n\u003c/tbody\u003e\n\u003c/table\u003e\u003c/markdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAs a general rule of thumb, we urge users of VIINA data to avoid variables for which the out-of-sample AUC is less than 0.80. Some additional caution is warranted here, since the randomly-selected data sample used to evaluate out-of-sample predictive accuracy has limited positive examples for some variables (e.g. \u003ccode\u003et_raid\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003et_occupy\u003c/code\u003e each have only one positive instance in this table).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWhile VIINA 1.0 will no longer be updated, the most recent version is available in archived form here:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/PreviousVersions/event_info_latest_v1.zip\"\u003eData/PreviousVersions/event_info_latest_v1.zip\u003c/a\u003e | Raw event reports (locations, dates, urls, headlines)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/PreviousVersions/event_labels_latest_v1.zip\"\u003eData/PreviousVersions/event_labels_latest_v1.zip\u003c/a\u003e | Event reports labeled by actor and tactic (from LSTM model)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/PreviousVersions/event_1pd_latest_v1.zip\"\u003eData/PreviousVersions/event_1pd_latest_v1.zip\u003c/a\u003e | De-duplicated event reports and labels (\"one-per-day\" filter)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThere are two versions of each variable included in the VIINA dataset:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col dir=\"auto\"\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePredicted probability that event belongs to each category, from the BERT model: Floating point, from 0 to 1.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eBinary indicators (ending with \"_b\"): binary integer, coded 0 or 1.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ol\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eWe selected thresholds for dichotomizing the predicted probabilities by maximizing the F1 score against a pre-labeled (out-of-sample) test set. The F1 score is equivalent to the harmonic mean of precision and recall, or TP/(TP + 1/2(FP+FN)), where TP is the number of true positives, FP is false positives, and FN is false negatives. For each variable, the algorithm considers every potential cutoff ranging from 0 to 1, compares the resulting binary values to \"true\" labels, calculates the F1 score, and selects the cutoff that maximizes this score. These cutoffs are different for each variable, and are enumerated in the table below.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eBelow are detailed out-of-same prediction accuracy statistics for each variable, along with the cutoffs for dichotomizing each variable (cutoff_01).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cmarkdown-accessiblity-table\u003e\u003ctable\u003e\n\u003cthead\u003e\n\u003ctr\u003e\n\u003cth fGqKFv"><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 eoaCFS js-snippet-clipboard-copy-unpositioned undefined" data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">VIINA 2.0 / Violent Incident Information from News Articles</h1><a id="user-content-viina-20--violent-incident-information-from-news-articles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: VIINA 2.0 / Violent Incident Information from News Articles" href="#viina-20--violent-incident-information-from-news-articles"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2022 Russian Invasion of Ukraine</h2><a id="user-content-2022-russian-invasion-of-ukraine" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2022 Russian Invasion of Ukraine" href="#2022-russian-invasion-of-ukraine"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/ctr_anim_latest.gif"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/ctr_anim_latest.gif" alt="Control" data-animated-image="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> (territorial control)</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/map_anim_latest.gif"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/map_anim_latest.gif" alt="All events" data-animated-image="" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> (events)</p>
<p dir="auto">VIINA/ВІЙНА/ВОЙНА/WAR 2.0 is a near-real time multi-source event data system for the 2022 Russian Invasion of Ukraine. These data are based on news reports from Ukrainian and Russian media, which were geocoded and classified into standard conflict event categories through machine learning. In addition to raw events, VIINA also includes data on territorial control, at the level of individual populated places.</p>
<p dir="auto">These data are GIS-ready, with temporal precision down to the minute. Each observation is accompanied by full source information, text and URLs.</p>
<p dir="auto">VIINA is updated daily, and is freely available for use by students, journalists, policymakers, and everyday researchers under an <a href="#open-data-commons-open-database-license">Open Database License (ODbL)</a>.</p>
<p dir="auto">The most recent versions these data are available as a comma-delimited-text (csv) files within the following compressed ZIP archives:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/control_latest_2022.zip">Data/control_latest_2022.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2022 (GeoNames locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/control_latest_2023.zip">Data/control_latest_2023.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2023 (GeoNames locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/control_latest_2024.zip">Data/control_latest_2024.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2024 (GeoNames locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/control_latest_2025.zip">Data/control_latest_2025.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2025 (GeoNames locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/kontrol_latest_2022.zip">Data/kontrol_latest_2022.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2022 (KATOTTH locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/kontrol_latest_2023.zip">Data/kontrol_latest_2023.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2023 (KATOTTH locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/kontrol_latest_2024.zip">Data/kontrol_latest_2024.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2024 (KATOTTH locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/kontrol_latest_2025.zip">Data/kontrol_latest_2025.zip</a> | Territorial control daily status for 2025 (KATOTTH locations)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2022.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2022.zip</a> | Raw event reports for 2022 (locations, dates, urls, headlines)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2023.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2023.zip</a> | Raw event reports for 2023 (locations, dates, urls, headlines)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2024.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2024.zip</a> | Raw event reports for 2024 (locations, dates, urls, headlines)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2025.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2025.zip</a> | Raw event reports for 2025 (locations, dates, urls, headlines)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2022.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2022.zip</a> | Event reports for 2022, labeled by actor and tactic (from BERT model)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2023.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2023.zip</a> | Event reports for 2023, labeled by actor and tactic (from BERT model)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2024.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2024.zip</a> | Event reports for 2024, labeled by actor and tactic (from BERT model)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2025.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2025.zip</a> | Event reports for 2025, labeled by actor and tactic (from BERT model)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2022.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2022.zip</a> | De-duplicated event reports and labels for 2022 ("one-per-day" filter)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2023.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2023.zip</a> | De-duplicated event reports and labels for 2023 ("one-per-day" filter)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2024.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2024.zip</a> | De-duplicated event reports and labels for 2024 ("one-per-day" filter)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2025.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2025.zip</a> | De-duplicated event reports and labels for 2025 ("one-per-day" filter)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Note that each event data release includes both raw event reports (<code>event_info</code>, <code>event_labels</code>) and a simplified, de-duplicated data file (<code>event_1pd</code>). The latter uses a "one-per-day" filter to remove potential duplicate event reports, by treating multiple event reports of the same type (i.e. same combination of actor and tactic labels) in the same populated place on the same day as a single unique event.</p>
<p dir="auto">Previous data versions are available by request (email me).</p>
<p dir="auto">Also included are tessellated geometries of Ukrainian populated places, which were used to create some of the maps on this site. These can be matched to the territorial control data by the variable <code>geonameid</code> (<code>control*</code> datasets) or <code>kod</code> (<code>kontrol*</code> datasets):</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/gn_UA_tess.geojson">Data/gn_UA_tess.geojson</a>  (N = 33,141 populated places)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/katotth_UA_tess.geojson">Data/katotth_UA_tess.geojson</a>  (N = 29,724 populated places)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">For additional information on VIINA (1.0) and illustrative analyses, see:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Zhukov, Yuri (2023). "Near-Real Time Analysis of War and Economic Activity during Russia’s Invasion of Ukraine." <em>Journal of Comparative Economics</em> 51 (4): 1232-1243 (<a href="https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jce.2023.06.003" rel="nofollow">doi.org/10.1016/j.jce.2023.06.003</a>). Offprint <a href="https://zhukovyuri.github.io/files/2023_Zhukov_JCE.pdf" rel="nofollow">available here</a>.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Please cite VIINA 2.0 data as:</p>
<ul dir="auto">

(<a href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA">https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA</a>, accessed [DATE]).</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Territorial Control Data</h2><a id="user-content-territorial-control-data" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Territorial Control Data" href="#territorial-control-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/map_ctr_latest.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/map_ctr_latest.png" alt="Current status" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">VIINA data on territorial control are based on four sources:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>VIINA event reports on territorial control</li>
<li>Polygon map layers from DeepStateMap (Ukraine)</li>
<li>Polygon map layers from Institute for the Study of War (U.S.)</li>
<li>Crowdsourced control maps from Wikipedia</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">In cases where these data sources disagree, a "majority vote" rule is used to determine whether a populated place is under the control of Ukrainian forces, Russian forces, or is being actively contested between the two. If these "votes" are evenly split, ties are broken in favor of DeepStateMap.</p>
<p dir="auto">Note that Institute for the Study of War (ISW) territorial control data are updated less frequently than the other three sources.</p>
<p dir="auto">Territorial control data are available for two sets of geographic units.
The first (<code>control</code>) includes full set of Ukrainian populated places in the <a href="https://www.geonames.org/" rel="nofollow">GeoNames gazetteer</a> (N = 33,141), with feature_code's beginning in PPL*.
The second (<code>kontrol</code>) uses Ukraine's national register of administrative divisions, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Codifier_of_administrative-territorial_units_and_territories_of_territorial_communities" rel="nofollow">KATOTTH</a> (N = 29,724), which can be more easily merged with official government statistics.</p>
<p dir="auto">Each territorial control dataset includes the following fields:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>geonameid</code> (in <code>control*</code> datasets only): Numeric ID of populated place (can be linked to geometries in <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/gn_UA_tess.geojson">gn_UA_tess.geojson</a>)</li>
<li><code>kod</code> (in <code>kontrol*</code> datasets only): KATOTTH code of populated place (can be linked to geometries in <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/katotth_UA_tess.geojson">katotth_UA_tess.geojson</a>)</li>
<li><code>date</code>: Date of map update (YYYYMMDD)</li>
<li><code>status_wiki</code>: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from Wikipedia crowdsourced maps</li>
<li><code>status_boost</code>: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from Wikipedia "boosted" by VIINA event reports</li>
<li><code>status_dsm</code>: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from DeepStateMap</li>
<li><code>status_isw</code>: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), from Institute for the Study of War</li>
<li><code>status</code>: Reported control status (UA/RU/CONTESTED), "majority vote" of wiki, boost and dsm</li>
<li><code>vcontrol_version</code>: Date and time of VIINA territorial control data release</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Note that the structure of these data have recently changed. Starting October 13, 2024, the data files are split by calendar year. Each yearly file follows the same "long" panel data format (rows are daily observations for each populated place, columns are control status from different sources).</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Event Data</h2><a id="user-content-event-data" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Event Data" href="#event-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>VIINA 2.0</strong> draws on news reports from the following Ukrainian and Russian news providers:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://24tv.ua/" rel="nofollow">24 Канал</a> ("24tvua"): Ukrainian 24 hour news network</li>
<li><a href="https://espreso.tv/" rel="nofollow">Espreso TV</a> ("espreso"): Ukrainian Internet TV station</li>
<li><a href="https://forbes.ua/" rel="nofollow">Forbes Ukraine</a> ("forbesua"): Ukrainian edition of Forbes magazine</li>
<li><a href="https://interfax.com.ua/" rel="nofollow">Інтерфакс-Україна</a> ("interfaxua"): Ukrainian affiliate of Russia's Interfax news wire service</li>
<li><a href="https://www.kp.ru/" rel="nofollow">Комсомольская Правда</a> ("kp"): Russian newspaper</li>
<li><a href="https://www.liga.net/" rel="nofollow">ЛІГА.net</a> ("liga"): Ukrainian internet news service</li>
<li><a href="https://liveuamap.com/" rel="nofollow">Live Universal Awareness Map</a> ("liveuamap"): Ukrainian conflict event mapping service</li>
<li><a href="https://mil.in.ua/uk/" rel="nofollow">Мілітарний</a> ("militarnyy"): Ukrainian defense news portal</li>
<li><a href="https://zona.media/" rel="nofollow">Медиазона</a> ("mz"): Russian news portal</li>
<li><a href="https://meduza.io/" rel="nofollow">Медуза</a> ("meduza"): Russian news portal</li>
<li><a href="https://nv.ua/ukr?utm_content=set_lang" rel="nofollow">НВ</a> ("nv"): Ukrainian magazine and internet news portal</li>
<li><a href="https://www.ng.ru/news/" rel="nofollow">Независимая Газета</a> ("ng"): Russian newspaper</li>
<li><a href="https://www.ntv.ru/novosti/" rel="nofollow">НТВ</a> ("ntv"): Russian television news</li>
<li><a href="https://www.pravda.com.ua/" rel="nofollow">Українська правда</a> ("pravdaua"): Ukrainian newspaper</li>
<li><a href="https://ria.ru/" rel="nofollow">РИА Новости</a> ("ria"): Russian news wire service</li>
<li><a href="https://www.unian.info/" rel="nofollow">УНІАН</a> ("unian"): Ukrainian news wire service</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">This set of sources may expand/change as the war unfolds -- due to interruptions to journalistic activity from military operations, cyber attacks, and state censorship, as well as the availability of new data from other information providers.</p>
<p dir="auto">Using an automated web scraping routine (which runs every 6 hours), VIINA extracts the text of news reports published by each source and their associated metadata (publication time and date, web urls). Using natural language processing, the system extracts and geocodes location names mentioned in each news item. A neural network model then classifies each event report into several pre-defined categories.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Geocoding</h2><a id="user-content-geocoding" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Geocoding" href="#geocoding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Events were geo-located by place names mentioned in the text of each news report, using APIs from Yandex and OpenStreetMaps. All unique geocoded locations were manually inspected for false positive and false negative matches.</p>
<p dir="auto">Geocoding precision ranges from street-level (<code>GEO_PRECISION="STREET"</code>) to province-level (<code>GEO_PRECISION="ADM1"</code>).</p>
<p dir="auto">Below is a map of <strong>all</strong> geocoded event reports since the start of Russia's military operations on February 24, 2022. Underneath the map is a timeline, showing the number of event reports published per day, across all data sources.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/map_all_latest.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/map_all_latest.png" alt="All events" title="All event reports, by location" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Time/time_all_latest.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Time/time_all_latest.png" alt="All events" title="All event reports, by time" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">Here is the subset of events under the category of "military operations" (<code>t_mil_b=1</code>):</p>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Maps/map_war_latest.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Maps/map_war_latest.png" alt="All events" title="Reports about military operations, by location" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/Time/time_1pd_all_latest.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/Time/time_1pd_all_latest.png" alt="All events" title="All event reports, with one-a-day filter" style="max-width: 100%;"></a> (all event types, one-per-day filter)

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Event classification</h2><a id="user-content-event-classification" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Event classification" href="#event-classification"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The data currently include the following event categories:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>t_mil</code>: Event is about war/military operations</li>
<li><code>t_loc</code>: Event report includes reference to specific location</li>
<li><code>t_san</code>: Event report mentions economic sanctions imposed on Russia</li>
<li><code>a_rus</code>: Event involves Russian or Russian-aligned armed forces</li>
<li><code>a_ukr</code>: Event involves Ukrainian or Ukrainian-aligned armed forces</li>
<li><code>a_rus_init</code>: Event initiated by Russian or Russian-aligned armed forces</li>
<li><code>a_ukr_init</code>: Event initiated by Ukrainian or Ukrainian-aligned armed forces</li>
<li><code>a_civ</code>: Event initiated by civilians</li>
<li><code>a_other</code>: Event initiated by a third party (e.g. U.S., EU, Red Cross)</li>
<li><code>t_aad</code>: Anti-air defense, Buk, shoulder-fired missiles (Igla, Strela, Stinger)</li>
<li><code>t_airstrike</code>: Air strike, strategic bombing, helicopter strike</li>
<li><code>t_uav</code>: Unmanned or remotely-piloted aerial vehicle</li>
<li><code>t_airalert</code>: Air raid siren/alert</li>
<li><code>t_armor</code>: Tank battle or assault</li>
<li><code>t_arrest</code>: Arrest by security services or detention of prisoners of war</li>
<li><code>t_artillery</code>: Shelling by field artillery, howitzer, mortar, or rockets like Grad/BM-21, Uragan/BM-27, other Multiple Launch Rocket System (MRLS)</li>
<li><code>t_control</code>: Establishment/claim of territorial control over population center</li>
<li><code>t_firefight</code>: Any exchange of gunfire with handguns, semi-automatic rifles, automatic rifles, machine guns, rocket-propelled grenades (RPGs)</li>
<li><code>t_ied</code>: Improvised explosive device, roadside bomb, landmine, car bomb, explosion</li>
<li><code>t_raid</code>: Assault/attack by paratroopers or special forces, usually followed by a retreat</li>
<li><code>t_occupy</code>: Occupation of territory or building</li>
<li><code>t_property</code>: Destruction of property or infrastructure</li>
<li><code>t_cyber</code>: Cyber operations, including DDOS attacks, website defacement</li>
<li><code>t_hospital</code>: Attacks on hospitals and humanitarian convoys</li>
<li><code>t_milcas</code>: Event report mentions military casualties</li>
<li><code>t_civcas</code>: Event report mentions civilian casualties</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">VIINA 2.0 uses a BERT-based transformer model (<a href="https://doi.org/10.48550/arXiv.1810.04805" rel="nofollow">Devlin, et al., 2018</a>) to classify news headlines into the above event categories. Transformers, first developed by Google in 2017, are a class of neural networks that can provide significant performance and efficiency gains over previous generations of recurrent neural networks (RNNs) and convolutional neural networks (CNNs) by using attention, which tracks relationships between elements of the data and enabling significant parallelization. One high-performing and widely-utilized transformer model is Bidirectional Encoder Representations from Transformers (BERT), developed by Google in 2018. This model uses only transformer encoder layers, whereas other models make use of both encoders and decoders, or only decoders.</p>
<p dir="auto">We employ an iteration of the BERT-base model, pre-trained using 12 transformer layers, 110 million parameters, and 3.3 billion words. Specifically, we use <a href="https://huggingface.co/KoichiYasuoka/bert-base-slavic-cyrillic-upos" rel="nofollow">KoichiYasouka's bert-base-slavic-cyrillic-upos model</a>, an iteration of the <a href="https://huggingface.co/ai-forever/ruBert-base" rel="nofollow">ruBERT</a>-base model trained on Belarusian, Bulgarian, Russian, Serbian, and Ukrainian texts for part-of-speech tasks. We fine-tune this model for classification using a labeled random subset of the Ukrainian and Russian news headlines scraped for VIINA and use the resulting fully-trained model to categorize all VIINA headlines.</p>
<p dir="auto">The previous version of VIINA (1.0) used an RNN model with long short-term memory (LSTM) (<a href="https://doi.org/10.1162/neco.1997.9.8.1735" rel="nofollow">Hochreiter and Schmidhuber, 1997</a>). LSTMs are well-suited for learning problems related to sequential data, such as sequences of words of differential length, where the vocabulary is potentially large, and where the long-term context and dependencies between inputs are potentially informative for classification (i.e. where word order and context matters, and the bag-of-words assumption is problematic).</p>
<p dir="auto">Below is a comparison of out-of-sample classification accuracy statistics --- areas under the Receiver-Operator Characteristic (AUC ROC) curves --- for the BERT (<code>roc_bert</code>) and LSTM (<code>roc_lstm</code>) models. These statistics can be interpreted as the probability that the model assigns a higher predicted probability to a randomly chosen event (e.g. <code>t_mil=1</code>) than to a randomly chosen non-event (e.g. <code>t_mil=0</code>). An AUC of 1 indicates perfect out-of-sample accuracy. An AUC of 0.50 indicates that a model performs no better than random classification. AUCs can be particularly useful in evaluating predictive performance for categories with high class imbalance (i.e. rare events, with a lot of 0's and very few 1's).</p>
<p dir="auto">As the table suggests, BERT universally dominates LSTM on this metric:</p>

<p dir="auto">As a general rule of thumb, we urge users of VIINA data to avoid variables for which the out-of-sample AUC is less than 0.80. Some additional caution is warranted here, since the randomly-selected data sample used to evaluate out-of-sample predictive accuracy has limited positive examples for some variables (e.g. <code>t_raid</code> and <code>t_occupy</code> each have only one positive instance in this table).</p>
<p dir="auto">While VIINA 1.0 will no longer be updated, the most recent version is available in archived form here:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/PreviousVersions/event_info_latest_v1.zip">Data/PreviousVersions/event_info_latest_v1.zip</a> | Raw event reports (locations, dates, urls, headlines)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/PreviousVersions/event_labels_latest_v1.zip">Data/PreviousVersions/event_labels_latest_v1.zip</a> | Event reports labeled by actor and tactic (from LSTM model)</li>
<li><a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/PreviousVersions/event_1pd_latest_v1.zip">Data/PreviousVersions/event_1pd_latest_v1.zip</a> | De-duplicated event reports and labels ("one-per-day" filter)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">There are two versions of each variable included in the VIINA dataset:</p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>Predicted probability that event belongs to each category, from the BERT model: Floating point, from 0 to 1.</li>
<li>Binary indicators (ending with "_b"): binary integer, coded 0 or 1.</li>
</ol>
<p dir="auto">We selected thresholds for dichotomizing the predicted probabilities by maximizing the F1 score against a pre-labeled (out-of-sample) test set. The F1 score is equivalent to the harmonic mean of precision and recall, or TP/(TP + 1/2(FP+FN)), where TP is the number of true positives, FP is false positives, and FN is false negatives. For each variable, the algorithm considers every potential cutoff ranging from 0 to 1, compares the resulting binary values to "true" labels, calculates the F1 score, and selects the cutoff that maximizes this score. These cutoffs are different for each variable, and are enumerated in the table below.</p>
<p dir="auto">Below are detailed out-of-same prediction accuracy statistics for each variable, along with the cutoffs for dichotomizing each variable (cutoff_01).</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">variable</th>
<th align="right">f1-score</th>
<th align="right">support</th>
<th align="right">accuracy</th>
<th align="right">roc-auc</th>
<th align="right">thresholds</th>
</tr>
</thead>

<p dir="auto">Note that these statistics are subject to change, as new events are added to the corpus and as the training set expands.</p>
<p dir="auto">Below are illustrative word clouds for several categories of events. The font size is proportional to word frequencies in news wire headlines predicted as being most likely to belong to each topic category (99th percentile of predicted probability). The clouds are for out-of-sample predictions on the full set of news stories in the corpus.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Events about war/military operations (t_mil_*)</h3><a id="user-content-events-about-warmilitary-operations-t_mil_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Events about war/military operations (t_mil_*)" href="#events-about-warmilitary-operations-t_mil_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/WC/wc_t_mil_test.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/WC/wc_t_mil_test.png" alt="wc_t_mil_test" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto">A quick guide to what some the words mean:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"окупанти" (okupanty) means "occupiers" (in Ukrainian)</li>
<li>"зсу" (zsu) is the acronym for Armed Forces of Ukraine (in Ukrainian)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Russian-initiated events (a_rus_*)</h3><a id="user-content-russian-initiated-events-a_rus_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Russian-initiated events (a_rus_*)" href="#russian-initiated-events-a_rus_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>"окупанти" (okupanty) means "occupiers"</li>
<li>"ворог" (voroh) means "enemy"</li>
<li>"війска" (viyska) means "forces"</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Ukrainian-initiated events (a_ukr_*)</h3><a id="user-content-ukrainian-initiated-events-a_ukr_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Ukrainian-initiated events (a_ukr_*)" href="#ukrainian-initiated-events-a_ukr_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>"зсу" (zsu) is the acronym for Armed Forces of Ukraine (in Ukrainian)</li>
<li>"всу" (vsu) is the acronym for Armed Forces of Ukraine (in Russian)</li>
<li>"заявили днр" (zayavili dnr) means "DNR has claimed" (in Russian)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Sanctions (t_san_*)</h3><a id="user-content-sanctions-t_san_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Sanctions (t_san_*)" href="#sanctions-t_san_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>"санкції" (sanktsiyi) means "sanctions"</li>

<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/WC/wc_t_firefight_test.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/WC/wc_t_firefight_test.png" alt="wc_t_mil_test" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"бої" (boyi) means "fighting" (in Ukrainian)</li>
<li>"бои" (boi) means "fighting" (in Russian)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Artillery shelling and rocket strikes (t_artillery_*)</h3><a id="user-content-artillery-shelling-and-rocket-strikes-t_artillery_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Artillery shelling and rocket strikes (t_artillery_*)" href="#artillery-shelling-and-rocket-strikes-t_artillery_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>"обстріл" (obstril) means "shelling"</li>
<li>"ракети" (rakety) means "rockets"</li>
<li>"заявили днр" (zayavili dnr) means "DNR has claimed" (i.e. allegations of shelling by UA forces in Donbas)</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Raid (t_raid_*)</h3><a id="user-content-raid-t_raid_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Raid (t_raid_*)" href="#raid-t_raid_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>"наступ" (nastup) means "advance/offensive"</li>
<li>"діверсантів" (diversantiv) means "of saboteurs/diversionary units"</li>
<li>"висадився десант" (vysadyvsya desant) means "paratroopers landed"</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Destruction of property or infrastructure (t_property_*)</h3><a id="user-content-destruction-of-property-or-infrastructure-t_property_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Destruction of property or infrastructure (t_property_*)" href="#destruction-of-property-or-infrastructure-t_property_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<ul dir="auto">
<li>"будинків" (budynkiv) means "houses"</li>
<li>"з під завалів" (z pid zavaliv) means "from under the rubble"</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cyber operations (t_cyber_*)</h3><a id="user-content-cyber-operations-t_cyber_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Cyber operations (t_cyber_*)" href="#cyber-operations-t_cyber_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Attacks on hospitals (t_hospital_*)</h3><a id="user-content-attacks-on-hospitals-t_hospital_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Attacks on hospitals (t_hospital_*)" href="#attacks-on-hospitals-t_hospital_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Military casualties (t_milcas_*)</h3><a id="user-content-military-casualties-t_milcas_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Military casualties (t_milcas_*)" href="#military-casualties-t_milcas_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Civilian casualties (t_civcas_*)</h3><a id="user-content-civilian-casualties-t_civcas_" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Civilian casualties (t_civcas_*)" href="#civilian-casualties-t_civcas_"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/blob/main/Figures/WC/wc_t_civcas_test.png"><img src="/zhukovyuri/VIINA/raw/main/Figures/WC/wc_t_civcas_test.png" alt="wc_t_mil_test" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>"поранені" (poraneni) means "wounded"</li>
<li>"людей" (lyudey) means "people"</li>
<li>"дітей" (ditey) means "children"</li>
<li>"цивільних" (tsyvil'nykh) means "civilian"</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Codebook</h2><a id="user-content-codebook" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Codebook" href="#codebook"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Raw event reports (<a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2022.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2022.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2023.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2023.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2024.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2024.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_info_latest_2025.zip">Data/event_info_latest_2025.zip</a>)</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>viina_version</code>: Date and time of VIINA data release</li>
<li><code>event_id</code>: Unique event ID</li>
<li><code>event_id_1pd</code>: De-duplicated event ID (from one-per-day filter)</li>
<li><code>date</code>: Date of event report (YYYYMMDD)</li>
<li><code>time</code>: Time of event report (HH:MM)</li>
<li><code>geonameid</code>: Numeric ID of populated place</li>
<li><code>feature_code</code>: Type of populated place (see <a href="https://www.geonames.org/export/codes.html" rel="nofollow">full list here</a>)</li>
<li><code>asciiname</code>: Name of populated place, ASCII values</li>
<li><code>ADM1_NAME</code>: Name of first-level administrative unit (oblast')</li>
<li><code>ADM1_CODE</code>: Numerical code of first-level administrative unit (oblast')</li>
<li><code>ADM2_NAME</code>: Name of second-level administrative unit (rayon)</li>
<li><code>ADM2_CODE</code>: Numerical code of second-level administrative unit (rayon)</li>
<li><code>longitude</code>: Longitude coordinate of event location</li>
<li><code>latitude</code>: Latitude coordinate of event location</li>
<li><code>GEO_PRECISION</code>: geographic precision of geocoded location</li>
<li><code>GEO_API</code>: Geocoding API used to locate event</li>
<li><code>location</code>: Index of unique locations mentioned in each event</li>
<li><code>address</code>: Address of geocoded location</li>
<li><code>report_id</code>: Unique ID for report that contains the event</li>
<li><code>source</code>: Data source short name</li>
<li><code>url</code>: URL web address of event report</li>
<li><code>text</code>: Text of event report headline/description</li>
<li><code>lang</code>: Language of report (ua is Ukrainian, ru is Russian)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">Event reports labeled by actor and tactic (<a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2022.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2022.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2023.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2023.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2024.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2024.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_labels_latest_2025.zip">Data/event_labels_latest_2025.zip</a>):</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>viina_version</code>: Date and time of VIINA data release</li>
<li><code>event_id</code>: Unique event ID</li>
<li><code>event_id_1pd</code>: De-duplicated event ID (from one-per-day filter)</li>
<li><code>date</code>: Date of event report (YYYYMMDD)</li>
<li><code>time</code>: Time of event report (HH:MM)</li>
<li><code>geonameid</code>: Numeric ID of populated place</li>
<li><code>t_[event type]</code>: Predicted probability (and binary indicator) that report describes event of each type (from BERT model, see above)</li>
<li><code>a_[actor]</code>: Predicted probability (and binary indicator) that report describes event initiated by each actor (from BERT model, see above)</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">De-duplicated event reports and labels (<a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2022.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2022.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2023.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2023.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2024.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2024.zip</a>, <a href="https://github.com/zhukovyuri/VIINA/tree/master/Data/event_1pd_latest_2025.zip">Data/event_1pd_latest_2025.zip</a>):</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>viina_version</code>: Date and time of VIINA data release</li>
<li><code>event_id_1pd</code>: De-duplicated event ID (from one-per-day filter)</li>
<li><code>date</code>: Date of event report (YYYYMMDD)</li>
<li><code>n_reports</code>: Number of constitutive event reports</li>
<li><code>event_ids</code>: IDs of constitutive events (<code>event_id</code> in above two files)</li>
<li><code>sources</code>: Sources for constitutive events (<code>source</code> in event_info_latest files)</li>
<li><code>geonameid</code>: Numeric ID of populated place</li>
<li><code>feature_code</code>: Type of populated place (see <a href="https://www.geonames.org/export/codes.html" rel="nofollow">full list here</a>)</li>
<li><code>asciiname</code>: Name of populated place, ASCII values</li>
<li><code>ADM1_NAME</code>: Name of first-level administrative unit (oblast')</li>
<li><code>ADM1_CODE</code>: Numerical code of first-level administrative unit (oblast')</li>
<li><code>ADM2_NAME</code>: Name of second-level administrative unit (rayon)</li>
<li><code>ADM2_CODE</code>: Numerical code of second-level administrative unit (rayon)</li>
<li><code>longitude</code>: Longitude coordinate of event location</li>
<li><code>latitude</code>: Latitude coordinate of event location</li>
<li><code>GEO_PRECISION</code>: geographic precision of geocoded location</li>
<li><code>t_[event type]</code>: Binary indicator for each event type (from BERT model, see above)</li>
<li><code>a_[actor]</code>: Binary indicator for each actor (from BERT model, see above)</li>
</ul>
